Great for those extra lazy moments in which you do not want to look for your keyboard, e.g. in the dark during movie-time.\r\n\r\n★ Typical Usage ★\r\n\r\n✔ During a movie you doze off, and do not want to risk being woken up by some action going on, e.g. a bit later on or by the next movie in your playlist.
